country_event = { #FR intervenes in Cabinet formation
	id = bobby.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bobby.5" }
	title = bobby.5.t
	desc = bobby.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_npp_generic_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept Burke_
		name = bobby.5.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 6 
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_RFK_MORAL_SHADOW option = USA_RFK_MORAL_SHADOW_CONSERVATIVE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { RFK_Liberalism = 1 }
			country_event = { id = bobby.6 days = 5 }
			remove_ideas = USA_Henry_Mucci_sec
			add_ideas = USA_Arleigh_Burke_sec
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_nat = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_nat }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_rep = 8 }
			add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_rep_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_rep }
		}
	}
	option = { #Dont
		name = bobby.5.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 4 
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_RFK_MORAL_SHADOW option = USA_RFK_MORAL_SHADOW_LIBERAL }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = bobby.7 days = 1 }
			set_country_flag = USA_rfk_c_boss
			add_to_variable = { RFK_Liberalism = 1 }
			set_country_flag = USA_RFK_deny_Burke
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		hidden_effect = {
			USA_HAR_fatigue_hit_1 = yes

			add_to_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_enthusiasm = 6 }

			subtract_from_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm = 8 }

			set_variable = { USA_L_NPP_bill_support_new = 0.2 } #Eat the rich
			set_variable = { USA_FR_NPP_bill_support_new = -0.05 } #So many people already hate this its hard to get more people to defect
			set_variable = { USA_RD_R_bill_support_new = -0.1 } #More people who support this initially hence a larger pool of defectors
			set_variable = { USA_RD_D_bill_support_new = -0.1 } #Same as NPP-FR

			USA_HAR_calculate_enthusiasm = yes
			USA_clamp_bill_support = yes

			set_country_flag = USA_HAR_more_taxes
		}
	}
